The EvaluationCoordinator monitors cluster position and signals\\n25: // when this node should start or stop evaluation:\\n26: //   - When a node becomes primary, its state cache is warmed from DB, then scheduler starts.\\n27: //   - When a node becomes secondary, evaluation stops and state cache is cleared.\\n28: //\\n29: // The scheduler is recreated on each promotion to primary.\\n30: type evaluationRunner struct {\\n31: \\tng      *AlertNG\\n32: \\tcancel  context.CancelFunc\\n33: \\tdone    chan error    // Receives error on crash, closed on clean exit\\n34: \\tstopped chan struct{} // Closed when goroutine exits (for Stop to wait)\\n35: }\\n36: \\n37: // startEvaluation starts the scheduler and state manager for alert rule evaluation.\\n38: func (r *evaluationRunner) startEvaluation(ctx context.Context) {\\n39: \\tif r.cancel != nil {\\n40: \\t\\treturn\\n41: \\t}\\n42: \\n43: \\t// Warm the state manager cache from the store before starting evaluation\\n44: \\t// to ensure we have the latest alert rule state in memory.\\n45: \\tr.ng.stateManager.Warm(ctx, r.ng.store, r.ng.store, r.ng.StartupInstanceReader)\\n46: \\tif r.ng.schedule == nil {\\n47: \\t\\tr.ng.schedule = schedule.NewScheduler(r.ng.schedCfg, r.ng.stateManager)\\n48: \\t}\\n49: \\n50: \\tschedCtx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\\n51: \\tr.cancel = cancel\\n52: \\tr.done = make(chan error, 1)\\n53: \\tr.stopped = make(chan struct{})\\n54: \\n55: \\t// Start the scheduler\\n56: \\tg, gCtx := errgroup.WithContext(schedCtx)\\n57: \\tg.Go(func() error {\\n58: \\t\\terr := r.ng.schedule.Run(gCtx)\\n59: \\t\\tif err == nil && gCtx.Err() == nil {\\n60: \\t\\t\\treturn fmt.Errorf(\\\"scheduler stopped unexpectedly\\\")\\n61: \\t\\t}\\n62: \\t\\treturn err\\n63: \\t})\\n64: \\n65: \\t// Start the state manager\\n66: \\tg.Go(func() error { return r.ng.stateManager.Run(gCtx) })\\n67: \\n68: \\t// Wait for scheduler and state manager to finish in background.\\n69: \\t// Signal errors via r.done, completion via r.stopped.\\n70: \\tgo func() {\\n71: \\t\\tdefer close(r.stopped)\\n72: \\t\\tdefer close(r.done)\\n73: \\t\\tif err := g.Wait(); err != nil && components:\\n\\n## Architecture Overview\\n\\nThe ngalert subsystem in pkg/services/ngalert/ implements a complete alert management pipeline consisting of five core components:\\n\\n### 1. Alert Rule Storage (pkg/services/ngalert/store/)\\nThe storage layer handles persistent alert rule data:\\n- **database.go (DBstore)**: Main database abstraction providing CRUD operations for alert rules\\n- **alert_rule.go**: Implements alert rule operations including DeleteAlertRulesByUID, GetAlertRulesForScheduling, and version management\\n- **alertmanager.go**: Manages alertmanager configuration persistence\\n- **instance_database.go**: Stores alert instance state transitions and history\\n- **models.go**: Data model serialization and conversions\\n\\nThe store uses optimistic locking (ErrOptimisticLock) and supports versioning for alert rule changes. It integrates with pkg/services/ngalert/models/ for core data structures like AlertRule and AlertInstance.\\n\\n### 2. Scheduler (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/)\\nThe scheduler coordinates periodic evaluation of alert rules:\\n- **schedule.go (ScheduleService)**: Main scheduler implementing the Run() method that orchestrates rule evaluation lifecycle. It uses a base interval timer and manages per-rule evaluation channels.\\n- **registry.go (ruleRegistry)**: Maintains an in-memory registry of rules being scheduled\\n- **alert_rule.go**: Handles individual alert rule scheduling logic\\n- **recording_rule.go**: Manages Prometheus recording rules\\n- **fetcher.go**: Fetches alert rules from storage for scheduling\\n\\nThe scheduler integrates with:\\n- State Manager (state/manager.go): Receives evaluation results\\n- Evaluator (eval/eval.go): Performs actual rule condition evaluation\\n- Rule Store (store/alert_rule.go): Retrieves rules to schedule\\n\\n### 3. State Manager (pkg/services/ngalert/state/)\\nTracks and persists alert instance state across evaluations:\\n- **manager.go (Manager)**: Core state management coordinating state transitions, caching, and persistence. Implements AlertInstanceManager interface\\n- **state.go (State)**: Represents individual alert instance state with timing information\\n- **cache.go**: In-memory state cache for fast lookups\\n- **persist.go (StatePersister)**: Interface for pluggable state persistence\\n- **persister_async.go**: Asynchronous state persistence with batching\\n- **persister_sync.go**: Synchronous state persistence for consistency\\n\\nThe state manager:\\n- Applies No-Data and Error handling logic\\n- Synchronizes state changes\\n- Triggers state transitions that are sent to historians and notifiers\\n- Maintains the cache from instance storage on startup\\n\\n### 4. History Writer (pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/)\\nRecords alert state changes over time through multiple backends:\\n- **core.go**: Utility functions ShouldRecord() and ShouldRecordAnnotation() determine which state transitions to persist\\n- **backend.go (backendHistorian)**: Generic pluggable history backend\\n- **annotation.go**: Records state changes as Grafana annotations (dashboard-visible)\\n- **loki.go (lokiHistorian)**: Writes state transitions to Loki for centralized logging\\n- **prometheus.go (prometheusHistorian)**: Writes state transitions to remote Prometheus via remote write API\\n- **dashboard.go**: Manages panel-level state history\\n\\nHistorians are triggered by state transitions and use StateTransition objects containing state changes, reasons, and timestamps.\\n\\n### 5. Notifier System (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/ and sender/)\\nManages notification routing and delivery:\\n\\n**Notifier (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/):**\\n- **alertmanager.go (alertmanager struct)**: Wraps the external alerting library's GrafanaAlertmanager with Grafana-specific state management\\n- **multiorg_alertmanager.go (MultiOrgAlertmanager)**: Manages per-organization alertmanager instances\\n- **alertmanager_config.go**: Handles alertmanager configuration persistence and updates\\n- **alerts.go (PutAlerts)**: Ingests alerts from the scheduler\\n- **alert_broadcast.go**: Broadcasts alerts to external systems\\n- **config.go**: Configuration parsing and validation\\n- **crypto.go**: Encrypts sensitive receiver credentials\\n\\n**Sender (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/):**\\n- **router.go (AlertsRouter)**: Routes alerts to external alertmanager instances\\n- **sender.go (ExternalAlertmanager)**: Manages HTTP delivery to external Alertmanager services with service discovery\\n- **notifier.go**: Adapter for notification sending\\n\\n### 6. Supporting Components\\n\\n**Evaluation Engine (pkg/services/ngalert/eval/):**\\n- **eval.go (ConditionEvaluator)**: Evaluates alert rule conditions against datasource queries and expressions\\n\\n**Metrics Writer (pkg/services/ngalert/writer/):**\\n- **prom.go (PromWriter)**: Writes evaluation results to remote Prometheus via remote write API\\n- **datasourcewriter.go**: Generic datasource-based metrics writer\\n\\n**API Layer (pkg/services/ngalert/api/):**\\n- **api.go**: Main API registration and routing\\n- **api_ruler.go**: Ruler-compatible API endpoints\\n- **api_provisioning.go**: Alert rule provisioning endpoints\\n- **api_alertmanager.go**: Alertmanager-compatible API endpoints\\n\\n**Main Service (pkg/services/ngalert/):**\\n- **ngalert.go (AlertNG)**: Top-level service implementing dependency injection via ProvideService(). Initializes and coordinates all subsystems.\\n- **evaluation_runner.go**: Manages evaluation lifecycle for HA single-node evaluation mode\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\nThe complete evaluation pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Schedule Start** (evaluation_runner.go:startEvaluation): Triggers scheduler and state manager startup\\n2. **Rule Fetching** (schedule/fetcher.go): Scheduler fetches alert rules from store (store/alert_rule.go:GetAlertRulesForScheduling)\\n3. **Rule Evaluation** (eval/eval.go:Evaluate): Evaluator executes queries and conditions\\n4. **State Update** (state/manager.go): Manager applies evaluation results to alert instances, detects state transitions\\n5. **Persistence** (state/persister_*.go): Async or sync persistence to database (instance_database.go)\\n6. **History Recording** (state/historian/): If ShouldRecord() returns true, transitions written to backends (Loki, Prometheus, annotations)\\n7. **Notification** (notifier/alertmanager.go): State changes trigger MultiOrgAlertmanager to route alerts\\n8. **External Delivery** (sender/router.go): AlertsRouter sends to external alertmanager instances via ExternalAlertmanager\\n9. **Metrics** (writer/prom.go): Optional metrics written to remote storage\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Interface-based abstraction**: Each component defines interfaces (ScheduleService, StatePersister, ConditionEvaluator) allowing pluggable implementations\\n- **Multi-org isolation**: MultiOrgAlertmanager maintains separate alertmanager instances per organization\\n- **Pluggable historians**: Multiple history backends can coexist (annotation, Loki, Prometheus)\\n- **State caching**: In-memory cache (state/cache.go) with persistent storage sync for performance\\n- **HA support**: evaluationRunner coordinates cluster-aware evaluation with single-node election\\n- **Configuration encryption**: Crypto layer protects receiver credentials in Notifier System (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/ and sender/)\\nManages notification routing and delivery:\\n\\n**Notifier (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/):**\\n- **alertmanager.go (alertmanager struct)**: Wraps the external alerting library's GrafanaAlertmanager with Grafana-specific state management\\n- **multiorg_alertmanager.go (MultiOrgAlertmanager)**: Manages per-organization alertmanager instances\\n- **alertmanager_config.go**: Handles alertmanager configuration persistence and updates\\n- **alerts.go (PutAlerts)**: Ingests alerts from the scheduler\\n- **alert_broadcast.go**: Broadcasts alerts to external systems\\n- **config.go**: Configuration parsing and validation\\n- **crypto.go**: Encrypts sensitive receiver credentials\\n\\n**Sender (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/):**\\n- **router.go (AlertsRouter)**: Routes alerts to external alertmanager instances\\n- **sender.go (ExternalAlertmanager)**: Manages HTTP delivery to external Alertmanager services with service discovery\\n- **notifier.go**: Adapter for notification sending\\n\\n### 6. Supporting Components\\n\\n**Evaluation Engine (pkg/services/ngalert/eval/):**\\n- **eval.go (ConditionEvaluator)**: Evaluates alert rule conditions against datasource queries and expressions\\n\\n**Metrics Writer (pkg/services/ngalert/writer/):**\\n- **prom.go (PromWriter)**: Writes evaluation results to remote Prometheus via remote write API\\n- **datasourcewriter.go**: Generic datasource-based metrics writer\\n\\n**API Layer (pkg/services/ngalert/api/):**\\n- **api.go**: Main API registration and routing\\n- **api_ruler.go**: Ruler-compatible API endpoints\\n- **api_provisioning.go**: Alert rule provisioning endpoints\\n- **api_alertmanager.go**: Alertmanager-compatible API endpoints\\n\\n**Main Service (pkg/services/ngalert/):**\\n- **ngalert.go (AlertNG)**: Top-level service implementing dependency injection via ProvideService(). Initializes and coordinates all subsystems.\\n- **evaluation_runner.go**: Manages evaluation lifecycle for HA single-node evaluation mode\\n\\n## Data Flow\\n\\nThe complete evaluation pipeline:\\n\\n1. **Schedule Start** (evaluation_runner.go:startEvaluation): Triggers scheduler and state manager startup\\n2. **Rule Fetching** (schedule/fetcher.go): Scheduler fetches alert rules from store (store/alert_rule.go:GetAlertRulesForScheduling)\\n3. **Rule Evaluation** (eval/eval.go:Evaluate): Evaluator executes queries and conditions\\n4. **State Update** (state/manager.go): Manager applies evaluation results to alert instances, detects state transitions\\n5. **Persistence** (state/persister_*.go): Async or sync persistence to database (instance_database.go)\\n6. **History Recording** (state/historian/): If ShouldRecord() returns true, transitions written to backends (Loki, Prometheus, annotations)\\n7. **Notification** (notifier/alertmanager.go): State changes trigger MultiOrgAlertmanager to route alerts\\n8. **External Delivery** (sender/router.go): AlertsRouter sends to external alertmanager instances via ExternalAlertmanager\\n9. **Metrics** (writer/prom.go): Optional metrics written to remote storage\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Interface-based abstraction**: Each component defines interfaces (ScheduleService, StatePersister, ConditionEvaluator) allowing pluggable implementations\\n- **Multi-org isolation**: MultiOrgAlertmanager maintains separate alertmanager instances per organization\\n- **Pluggable historians**: Multiple history backends can coexist (annotation, Loki, Prometheus)\\n- **State caching**: In-memory cache (state/cache.go) with persistent storage sync for performance\\n- **HA support**: evaluationRunner coordinates cluster-aware evaluation with single-node election\\n- **Configuration encryption**: Crypto layer protects receiver credentials in storage\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
